# Manual Benchmark Data Import to Railway Production

## Instructions for Manual Import

### Option 1: Railway Database Console (Recommended)

1. **Access Railway Dashboard:**
   - Go to: https://railway.app/dashboard
   - Select your project: `alert-celebration` 
   - Select service: `ProfessionalSide`
   - Go to the Database tab
   - Click "Connect" or "Query"

2. **Copy and paste this SQL statement:**

```sql
INSERT INTO "SkillBenchmark" (id, "skillName", industry, role, "industryAverage", "juniorLevel", "midLevel", "seniorLevel", "expertLevel", "marketDemand", "growthTrend", description, "createdAt", "updatedAt") VALUES
  ('cmfdju5am003ku6ez9tbrm1e3', '360-Degree Feedback Systems', 'general', 'general', 58, 29, 44, 64, 76, 'medium', 'stable', 'Uncategorized skill with medium market demand and stable growth trend. Industry benchmark based on market analysis and role requirements.', '2025-09-10T05:38:44.686Z', '2025-09-10T05:38:44.686Z'),
  -- [FULL SQL CONTENT TO BE PROVIDED BELOW]
```

3. **Expected Result:**
   - Should insert 976 benchmark records
   - Each record contains: skill name, industry averages, level benchmarks, market demand, growth trend

### Option 2: Railway CLI with psql

If you have PostgreSQL client installed locally:

1. Get the DATABASE_URL:
```bash
railway run -- node -e "console.log(process.env.DATABASE_URL)"
```

2. Execute the SQL file:
```bash
psql "YOUR_DATABASE_URL_HERE" < migration.sql
```

### Verification Query

After import, verify with:
```sql
SELECT COUNT(*) as total_benchmarks FROM "SkillBenchmark";
SELECT "skillName", "industryAverage", "marketDemand", "growthTrend" 
FROM "SkillBenchmark" 
ORDER BY "skillName" 
LIMIT 5;
```

Expected: 976 total benchmarks
